20#[allow(dead_code)]
21pub mod util {
22    use core::result::Result::{Ok, Err};
23
24    pub fn bsearch_range_value_table<T: Copy>(c: char, r: &'static [(char, char, T)]) -> Option<T> {
25        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
26        match r.binary_search_by(|&(lo, hi, _)| {
27            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
28            else if hi < c { Less }
29            else { Greater }
30        }) {
31            Ok(idx) => {
32                let (_, _, cat) = r[idx];
33                Some(cat)
34            }
35            Err(_) => None
36        }
37    }
38
39}

110    /// Groupings of the most general classification of a character.

130        super::util::bsearch_range_value_table(c, GENERAL_CATEGORY).unwrap_or(GeneralCategory::Unassigned)

133    #[inline]
134    pub(crate) fn general_category_is_letter_cased(gc: GeneralCategory) -> bool {
135        matches!(gc, GeneralCategory::UppercaseLetter | GeneralCategory::LowercaseLetter | GeneralCategory::TitlecaseLetter)
136    }

138    #[inline]
139    pub(crate) fn general_category_group(gc: GeneralCategory) -> GeneralCategoryGroup {
140        match gc {
141            GeneralCategory::UppercaseLetter |
142            GeneralCategory::LowercaseLetter |
143            GeneralCategory::TitlecaseLetter |
144            GeneralCategory::ModifierLetter |
145            GeneralCategory::OtherLetter => GeneralCategoryGroup::Letter,
146            GeneralCategory::NonspacingMark |
147            GeneralCategory::SpacingMark |
148            GeneralCategory::EnclosingMark => GeneralCategoryGroup::Mark,
149            GeneralCategory::DecimalNumber |
150            GeneralCategory::LetterNumber |
151            GeneralCategory::OtherNumber => GeneralCategoryGroup::Number,
152            GeneralCategory::ConnectorPunctuation |
153            GeneralCategory::DashPunctuation |
154            GeneralCategory::OpenPunctuation |
155            GeneralCategory::ClosePunctuation |
156            GeneralCategory::InitialPunctuation |
157            GeneralCategory::FinalPunctuation |
158            GeneralCategory::OtherPunctuation => GeneralCategoryGroup::Punctuation,
159            GeneralCategory::MathSymbol |
160            GeneralCategory::CurrencySymbol |
161            GeneralCategory::ModifierSymbol |
162            GeneralCategory::OtherSymbol => GeneralCategoryGroup::Symbol,
163            GeneralCategory::SpaceSeparator |
164            GeneralCategory::LineSeparator |
165            GeneralCategory::ParagraphSeparator => GeneralCategoryGroup::Separator,
166            GeneralCategory::Control |
167            GeneralCategory::Format |
168            GeneralCategory::Surrogate |
169            GeneralCategory::PrivateUse |
170            GeneralCategory::Unassigned => GeneralCategoryGroup::Other,
171        }
172    }

2792
2793#[cfg(feature = "emoji")]
2794pub mod emoji {
2795
2796    #[derive(Copy, Clone, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, Ord, PartialOrd, Debug)]
2797    #[non_exhaustive]
2798    /// The emoji character properties of a character.
2799    pub enum EmojiStatus {
2800        /// `Emoji=NO`, `Emoji_Component=NO`
2801        NonEmoji,
2802        /// `Emoji=NO`, `Emoji_Component=YES`
2803        NonEmojiButEmojiComponent,
2804        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=NO`;`Emoji_Presentation=YES`
2805        EmojiPresentation,
2806        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=NO`;`Emoji_Modifier_Base=YES`
2807        EmojiModifierBase,
2808        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=NO`;`Emoji_Presentation=YES`, `Emoji_Modifier_Base=YES`
2809        EmojiPresentationAndModifierBase,
2810        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=NO`
2811        EmojiOther,
2812        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=YES`;`Emoji_Presentation=YES`
2813        EmojiPresentationAndEmojiComponent,
2814        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=YES`;`Emoji_Presentation=YES`, `Emoji_Modifier=YES`
2815        EmojiPresentationAndModifierAndEmojiComponent,
2816        /// `Emoji=YES`, `Emoji_Component=YES`
2817        EmojiOtherAndEmojiComponent,
2818    }
2819    #[inline]
2820    pub(crate) fn emoji_status(c: char) -> EmojiStatus {
2821        // FIXME: do we want to special case ASCII here?
2822        super::util::bsearch_range_value_table(c, EMOJI_STATUS).unwrap()
2823    }
2824    #[inline]
2825    pub(crate) fn is_emoji_status_for_emoji_char_or_emoji_component(s: EmojiStatus) -> bool {
2826        !matches!(s, EmojiStatus::NonEmoji)
2827    }
2828    #[inline]
2829    pub(crate) fn is_emoji_status_for_emoji_char(s: EmojiStatus) -> bool {
2830        !matches!(s, EmojiStatus::NonEmoji | EmojiStatus::NonEmojiButEmojiComponent)
2831    }
2832    #[inline]
2833    pub(crate) fn is_emoji_status_for_emoji_component(s: EmojiStatus) -> bool {
2834        matches!(s, EmojiStatus::EmojiPresentationAndEmojiComponent |
2835            EmojiStatus::EmojiPresentationAndModifierAndEmojiComponent |
2836            EmojiStatus::EmojiOtherAndEmojiComponent)
2837    }
